until\\n241:      * authentication succeeds or fails.\\n242:      *\\n243:      * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\\n244:      * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\\n245:      */\\n246:     @SuppressWarnings(\\\"fallthrough\\\")\\n247:     @Override\\n248:     public void authenticate() throws IOException {\\n249:         if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\\n250:             if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\\n251:                 return;\\n252: \\n253:             if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\\n254:                 setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\\n255:                 return;\\n256:             }\\n257: \\n258: connectionId);\\n260: \\n261:             try {\\n262:                 netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\\n263:             } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\\n264:                 throw new      break;\\n285:                     // For default GSSAPI, fall through to authenticate using the client token as the first GSSAPI packet.\\n286:                     // This is required for interoperability with 0.9.0.x clients which do not send handshake request\\n287:                 case AUTHENTICATE:\\n288:                     handleSaslToken(clientToken);\\n289:                     // When the authentication exchange is complete and no more tokens are expected from the client,\\n290:                     // update SASL state. }\\n335: \\n336:     @Override\\n337:     public void close() throws IOException {\\n338:         if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\\n339:             Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\\n442:             RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\\n443: // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\\n451:                 throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\\\"Version \\\" + version + \\n504:     private boolean handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\\n505:         boolean isKafkaRequest = false;\\n506:         String clientMechanism = null;\\n507:         try {\\n508:             ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\\n509:             RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\\n510:             ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\\n511: \\n512:             // A valid Kafka request header was received. This avoids\\n519:             // unnecessary exposure to some of the more complex schema types.\\n520:             if (apiKey != ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS && apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_HANDSHAKE)\\n521:                 throw new IllegalSaslStateException(\\\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \\\" + apiKey + \\\" during SASL handshake.\\\");\\n522: \\n523:             LOG.debug(\\\"Handling Kafka request {} during {}\\\", apiKey, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\\n524: \\n525: \\n526:             RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\\n527:                     KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\\n528:             RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\\n529:             if (apiKey == ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS)\\n530:                 handleApiVersionsRequest(requestContext, (ApiVersionsRequest) requestAndSize.request);\\n531:             else\\n532:                 clientMechanism = handleHandshakeRequest(requestContext, (SaslHandshakeRequest) requestAndSize.request);\\n533:         } catch (InvalidRequestException e) {\\n534:             if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST) {\\n535:                 // InvalidRequestException is thrown if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key\\n536:                 // is invalid. (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\\n539:                     StringBuilder tokenBuilder = new StringBuilder();\\n540:                     for (byte b : requestBytes) {\\n541:                         tokenBuilder.append(String.format(\\\"%02x\\\", b));\\n542:                         if (tokenBuilder.length() >= 20)\\n543:                              break;\\n544:                     }\\n545:                     LOG.debug(\\\"Received client packet of length {} starting with bytes 0x{}, process as GSSAPI packet\\\", requestBytes.length, tokenBuilder);\\n546:                 }\\n547: UnsupportedSaslMechanismException(\\\"Exception handling first SASL packet from client, GSSAPI is not supported by server\\\", e);\\n552:             } else\\n553:                 throw e;\\n554: handleHandshakeRequest(RequestContext context, SaslHandshakeRequest handshakeRequest) throws IOException, UnsupportedSaslMechanismException {\\n564:         String clientMechanism = handshakeRequest.data().mechanism();\\n565:         short version = context.header.apiVersion();\\n566:         if (version >= 1)\\n567:             this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(true);\\n568:         if (enabledMechanisms.contains(clientMechanism)) {\\n569:             LOG.debug(\\\"Using SASL mechanism '{}' provided by client\\\",
